C.H. and I.F. contributed to the lipidomic analysis. G.F.V. provided support for MSI experiments. J.M.D. and B.S. identified and collected plant material and conducted seed staging for experiments. L.B. and E.M. performed the whole seed nuclear magnetic resonance analyses. D.S., S.L., Z.-W.Z., Y.S., K.D.C., L.-L.C., and L.G. drafted the manuscript with input from other authors. All authors read and approved the manuscript. <strong>Competing interests:</strong> The authors declare that they have no competing interests. <strong>Data and materials availability:</strong> All data needed to evaluate the conclusions in the paper are present in the paper and/or the Supplementary Materials. Additional data related to this paper may be requested from the authors. The jojoba genome assembly and meta-data were deposited in the genome warehouse in Beijing Institute of Genomics (BIG) data center, BIG under accession no. GWHAASQ00000000 that is publicly accessible at <a href="http://bigd.big.ac.cn/gwh">http://bigd.big.ac.cn/gwh</a>. RNA-seq transcriptomic data were deposited to NCBI GEO repository and can be accessed using accession no. GSE130603.</div><ul class="copyright-statement"><li class="fn" id="copyright-statement-1">Copyright © 2020 The Authors, some rights reserved; exclusive licensee American Association for the Advancement of Science.   <div class="primary"><h2 class="subsection-title heading--block"><a href="https://science.sciencemag.org/content/current" target="_blank">Read the Latest Issue of <em>Science</em></a></h2>
  <div class="primary__main promo-foot--mag"><div class="promo-foot--current">
  
        
      <div class="highwire-article-citation highwire-citation-type-highwire-issue" data-pisa="sci;371/6526" data-pisa-master="sci;371/6526" data-apath="/sci/371/6526.atom" id="sci3716526atom"><h3>15 January 2021</h3>
<p class="promo-foot__meta">Vol 371, Issue 6526</p>
<a href="https://science.sciencemag.org/content/current" target="_blank" class="" data-icon-position="" data-hide-link-title="0"><img class="promo-foot__cover" src="https://advances.sciencemag.org/sites/default/files/styles/sci_footer_promo_cover/public/externals/14067c1c7f0ec4e8744a44035d73cebe.gif?itok=-W1DANw0" alt="Magazine Cover" /></a></div><p><a href="http://science.sciencemag.org/content/371/6526" class="btn--cta btn--cta--small" data-icon-position="" data-hide-link-title="0">Table of Contents</a></p>  
</div>
<div class="promo-foot--heds">
  
        
      <ul class="media-grid media-grid--2 media-grid--minor"><li class="first"><div class="highwire-article-citation highwire-citation-type-highwire-article" data-pisa="sci;371/6526/225" data-pisa-master="sci;371/6526/225" data-apath="/sci/371/6526/225.atom" id="sci3716526225atom"><h3 class="overline">Feature</h3>
  <a href="http://science.sciencemag.org/content/371/6526/225" class="highwire-cite-linked-title" data-icon-position="" data-hide-link-title="0"><span class="highwire-cite-title">Fallen giant</span></a></div></li>
<li><div class="highwire-article-citation highwire-citation-type-highwire-article" data-pisa="sci;371/6526/239" data-pisa-master="sci;371/6526/239" data-apath="/sci/371/6526/239.atom" id="sci3716526239atom"><h3 class="overline">Biodiversity</h3>
  <a href="http://science.sciencemag.org/content/371/6526/239" class="highwire-cite-linked-title" data-icon-position="" data-hide-link-title="0"><span class="highwire-cite-title">Tracking, targeting, and conserving soil biodiversity</span></a></div></li>
<li><div class="highwire-article-citation highwire-citation-type-highwire-article" data-pisa="sci;371/6526/242" data-pisa-master="sci;371/6526/242" data-apath="/sci/371/6526/242.atom" id="sci3716526242atom"><h3 class="overline">Climate Science</h3>
  <a href="http://science.sciencemag.org/content/371/6526/242" class="highwire-cite-linked-title" data-icon-position="" data-hide-link-title="0"><span class="highwire-cite-title">Fighting the good fight</span></a></div></li>
<li><div class="highwire-article-citation highwire-citation-type-highwire-article" data-pisa="sci;371/6526/216" data-pisa-master="sci;371/6526/216" data-apath="/sci/371/6526/216.atom" id="sci3716526216atom"><h3 class="overline">SCI COMMUN</h3>
  <a href="http://science.sciencemag.org/content/371/6526/216" class="highwire-cite-linked-title" data-icon-position="" data-hide-link-title="0"><span class="highwire-cite-title">News at a glance</span></a></div></li>
<li><div class="highwire-article-citation highwire-citation-type-highwire-article" data-pisa="sci;371/6526/230" data-pisa-master="sci;371/6526/230" data-apath="/sci/371/6526/230.atom" id="sci3716526230atom"><h3 class="overline">Coronavirus</h3>
  <a href="http://science.sciencemag.org/content/371/6526/230" class="highwire-cite-linked-title" data-icon-position="" data-hide-link-title="0"><span class="highwire-cite-title">Herd immunity by infection is not an option</span></a></div></li>
<li class="last"><div class="highwire-article-citation highwire-citation-type-highwire-article" data-pisa="sci;371/6526/314" data-pisa-master="sci;371/6526/314" data-apath="/sci/371/6526/314.atom" id="sci3716526314atom"><h3 class="overline">Working Life</h3>
  <a href="http://science.sciencemag.org/content/371/6526/314" class="highwire-cite-linked-title" data-icon-position="" data-hide-link-title="0"><span class="highwire-cite-title">No use in shouting</span></a></div></li>
